When I got off the taxi at the hotel, Master Zhong, who was very enthusiastic, helped me take my luggage to the front desk to check in. Thank him very much! msg:This time I went back to Nanjing and chose "Nanjing Shangri-La Hotel" among the many five-star hotels. Firstly, because I have always had a good impression of the Shangri-La brand; secondly, because of its superior geographical location. Facts prove that the choice is correct [strong]
        First of all, it is located on the north bank of Xuanwu Lake. Turn left when you go out and you will reach the Xuanwu Lake Tunnel. The main roads from east to west, north and south meet here, which can be said to be connected in all directions. Because it is not far from the main attractions, we stopped driving after staying at the hotel (the underground parking lot is free for hotel guests) and took a taxi (the taxi is very easy to hail). It was very convenient to get in and out.
        Secondly, the environment is quite beautiful, despite being located in a downtown area. It has an independent small garden with red flowers and green grass; it only takes 5 minutes to walk to the Xuanwu Lake; you can see the lake and mountains (Purple Mountain) from the high-rise buildings on the side of the lake.
        Again, it feels very comfortable to live in. We stayed in a lake-view king room on the 22nd floor. It was quite large and had good sound insulation. The room could be partitioned off with a sliding door to form a one-bedroom-one-living room. The huge floor-to-ceiling windows faced the lake (slightly blocked), and the view was wide and quiet. .
        The entire hotel's catering should also be a strong point: there are five restaurants of different styles on the first, second, fifth, and two floors above the 40th floor. The dinner in the buffet restaurant on the second floor is very cost-effective; the large terrace next to the hot pot restaurant on the fifth floor is impressive; the VIP lounge on the 40th floor has a first-class view and a rich wine list.
        Of course, what impressed me the most was Shangri-La‚Äôs service: due to an unexpected situation, I was able to witness the efficient communication and professionalism between the front office, catering depar**ent, and guest room depar**ent. It was gratifying and admirableüëç, and showed the relationship with The service level is consistent with the brand image.
        Overall, satisfied [strong]!

Facilities: Shangri-La's hardware facilities are still very good. The slippers don't have a foamy smell like other hotels, and there is no smell at all, which is very comfortable. The hotel has a total of 42 floors, and several elevators are dispatched very quickly, so there is basically no need to wait. There are not many people on the Internet celebrity apron on the top floor to check in, and it is not particularly popular. You can take a look at the Nanjing city view and take a photo to check in. What needs to be mentioned is that you have to take the elevator to the 42nd floor and then climb 3 flights of stairs. It is not convenient for those with legs or feet. Don't go if you have heart disease.

Service: There are two bottles of juice, two bottles of beer, and two bottles of Sprite Coke in the mini bar in the refrigerator. The first round is free, which were not stated when booking. The service attitude is still pretty good, there is a
The girl who checked in and the girl in the coffee bar were not very happy. The check-in time was too long, because the room has not been cleaned up. Let us go to the Horizon Club for afternoon tea. In fact, the room was not full that day, why bother? wait?

The hotel's buffet breakfast is very good. When you enter the restaurant, a waiter will guide you to your seat and ask if you want coffee or black tea. This experience is very good, and there are many varieties. There are many Chinese and Western styles. The fruits are fresh and the juice is freshly squeezed. Duck vermicelli soup and Xiaolongbao have the most queues, and the taste is also good, which is very satisfying.

It seems that there is nothing special about booking Shangri-La on Ctrip, and there is no record of membership points for Shangri-La. It seems to be cheaper to book on your own app, and there are all the services you should have. Next time, I will book with the app.

msg:Bringing children to experience the historical and cultural a**osphere of Nanjing's ancient capital, choosing to stay in Shangri-La, is a worthwhile trip. First of all, the hotel has convenient transportation. When you enter the city, you can go through the Xuanwu Lake Tunnel. The subway line 1 is just downstairs, so it is convenient to go anywhere. Secondly, the hotel environment is very good. You can enjoy the panoramic view of Xuanwu Lake from the room, overlooking the distance The beautiful scenery of Zijin Mountain, with mountains and water, has a panoramic view. Downstairs there is the hotel's own small garden. It's good to take a walk in the evening to digest food. Finally, the hotel service staff is warm and friendly. Every time they meet a guest, they will take the initiative to say hello, greet them with a smile, and respond to every request. The front desk service staff suggested that we upgrade the room type. We can enjoy the breakfast service of the VIP Pavilion on the 40th floor, afternoon tea and evening mini bar service. In the afternoon, we can sit in the coffee bar on the 40th floor, read books, drink tea, and enjoy the scenery. It is very comfortable. This The upgrade is well worth it. Here, I would like to thank the hotel staff Miao Qiqin, Liu Jiumin, Yang Dan, Yu Xiang and Wu Tong. This time I stayed for three nights in a row, and the sanitation was in place every night.
